list[list[DataFlowNode]]:\n   125→        \"\"\"Detect cycles using iterative DFS with coloring.\n   126→\n   127→        Returns list of cycles found (each cycle is a list of nodes).\n   128→        \"\"\"\n   129→        WHITE, GRAY, BLACK = 0, 1, 2\n   130→        color: dict[DataFlowNode, int] = {n: WHITE for n in self.nodes}\n   131→        parent: dict[DataFlowNode, DataFlowNode | None] = {}\n   132→        cycles: list[list[DataFlowNode]] = []\n   133→\n   134→        for start in self.nodes:\n   135→            if color[start] != WHITE:\n   136→                continue\n   137→\n   138→            stack: list[tuple[DataFlowNode, int]] = [(start, 0)]\n   139→            parent[start] = None\n   140→\n   141→            while stack:\n   142→                node, edge_idx = stack[-1]\n   143→\n   144→                if color[node] == WHITE:\n   145→                    color[node] = GRAY\n   146→\n   147→                outgoing = self._adjacency.get(node, [])\n   148→    if color[neighbor] == GRAY:\n   153→                        # Found a cycle -- reconstruct\n   154→                        cycle = [neighbor]\n   155→                        for s_node, _ in           cycles.append(list(reversed(cycle)))\n   160→                    elif color[neighbor] == WHITE:\n   161→                        parent[neighbor] = node\n   162→                        stack.append((neighbor, 0))\n   163→                else:\n   164→                    color[node] = BLACK\n   165→                    stack.pop()\n   166→\n   167→        return cycles\n   168→\n with no subsequent read edge.\n   173→        \"\"\"\n   174→        dead: list[DataFlowNode] = []\n   175→        for node in self.nodes:\n   176→            if node.operation in Contradiction indicators\n   103→_POSITIVE_INDICATORS = {\"delivered\", \"processed\", \"completed\", \"sent\", \"written\", \"all\", \"total\"}\n   104→_NEGATIVE_INDICATORS = {\"undelivered\", \"unprocessed\", \"pending\", \"remaining\", \"failed\", \"none\"}\n   105→\n   106→\n   107→def _tokenize(text: str) -> set[str]:\n   108→    \"\"\"Tokenize text into lowercase words.\"\"\"\n   109→ mismatch: one side says 'all/total', other says 'filtered/subset'.\"\"\"\n   114→    writer_has_all = bool(writer_tokens & _SCOPE_ALL)\n   115→    writer_has_filtered = bool(writer_tokens & _SCOPE_FILTERED)\n   116→    reader_has_all = bool(reader_tokens & _SCOPE_ALL)\n   117→    reader_has_filtered = bool(reader_tokens & _SCOPE_FILTERED)\n   118→\n   119→    return (writer_has_all and reader_has_filtered) or (writer_has_filtered and reader_has_all)\n   120→\n   121→\n   122→def _detect_type_mismatch(writer_tokens: set[str], reader_tokens: set[str]) -> bool:\n   123→    \"\"\"Detect type mismatch: writer implies one type, reader implies another.\"\"\"\n   124→    for i, group_a in enumerate(_TYPE_GROUPS):\n   125→        for group_b in _TYPE_GROUPS[i + 1:]:\n   126→ reader_in_a = bool(reader_tokens & group_a)\n   130→            if (writer_in_a and reader_in_b) or (writer_in_b and reader_in_a):\n   131→                return True\n   132→    return False\n   133→\n   134→\n   135→def _detect_direct_contradiction(writer_tokens: set[str], reader_tokens: set[str]) -> bool:\n   136→    \"\"\"Detect direct contradiction: writer says positive, reader says negative or vice versa.\"\"\"\n   137→    writer_pos = bool(writer_tokens & _POSITIVE_INDICATORS)\n   138→    writer_neg = bool(writer_tokens & _NEGATIVE_INDICATORS)\n   139→    reader_pos = -> bool:\n   150→    \"\"\"Detect completeness mismatch using semantic and invariant cross-reference.\"\"\"\n   151→    # Check for partial vs complete indicators\n   152→    completeness_full = {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"call_SHpwUH2t2njNWZRxT51tW299","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→\"\"\"Pipeline executor -- generic step sequencer with retry, gates, and parallel dispatch.\n     2→\n     3→Composition-via-callable design: consumers (sprint, roadmap) inject their own\n     4→StepRunner and callbacks. The executor handles step ordering, retry logic,\n     5→parallel dispatch, and state management.\n     6→\n     7→NFR-007: No imports from superclaude.cli.sprint or superclaude.cli.roadmap.\n     8→\"\"\"\n     9→\n    10→from __future__ import annotations\n    11→\n    12→import logging\n    13→import threading\n    14→from datetime import datetime, timezone\n    15→from typing import Callable, Protocol\n    16→\n    17→from .gates import gate_passed\n    18→from .models import PipelineConfig, Step, StepResult, StepStatus\n    19→\n    20→_log = logging.getLogger(\"superclaude.pipeline.executor\")\n    21→\n    22→\n    23→class StepRunner(Protocol):\n    24→    \"\"\"Callable that executes a single step's subprocess and returns a result.\n    25→\n    26→    The runner is responsible for:\n    27→    - Launching the claude -p subprocess\n    28→    - Waiting for completion (with timeout enforcement)\n    29→    - Returning a StepResult with appropriate status\n    30→\n    31→    The runner is NOT responsible for:\n    32→    - Retry logic (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    33→    - Gate checking (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    34→    - Step ordering (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    35→    \"\"\"\n    36→\n    37→    def __call__(\n    38→        self,\n    39→        step: Step,\n    40→        config: PipelineConfig,\n    41→        cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n    42→    ) -> StepResult: ...\n    43→\n    44→\n    45→def execute_pipeline(\n    46→    steps: list[Step | list[Step]],\n    47→    config: PipelineConfig,\n    48→    run_step: StepRunner,\n    49→    on_step_start: Callable[[Step], None] = lambda s: None,\n    50→    on_step_complete: Callable[[Step, StepResult], None] = lambda s, r: None,\n    51→    on_state_update: Callable[[dict], None] = lambda state: None,\n    52→    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool] = lambda: False,\n    53→) -> list[StepResult]:\n    54→    \"\"\"Generic pipeline executor.\n    55→\n    56→    Processes steps in order. Each element in ``steps`` is either:\n    57→    - A single Step (executed sequentially)\n    58→    - A list[Step] (all steps in the list executed in parallel)\n    59→\n    60→    For each step:\n    61→    1. Call on_step_start(step)\n    62→    2. Call run_step(step, config, cancel_check)\n    63→    3. If step has gate criteria: run gate_passed()\n    64→    4. If gate fails and attempts < retry_limit: retry (go to 2)\n    65→    5. If gate fails and attempts exhausted: HALT\n    66→    6. Call on_step_complete(step, result)\n    67→    7. Call on_state_update(updated_state_dict)\n    68→\n    69→    For parallel step groups:\n    70→    - All steps in the group run concurrently via _run_parallel_steps()\n    71→    - If any step in the group fails, remaining steps are cancelled\n    72→    - All results from the group must be PASS before proceeding\n    73→\n    74→    Returns list of all StepResults (one per step, flattened).\n    75→    \"\"\"\n    76→    all_results: list[StepResult] = []\n    77→\n    78→    for entry in steps:\n    79→        if cancel_check():\n    80→            break\n    81→\n    82→        if isinstance(entry, list):\n    83→            # Parallel step group\n    84→            for s in entry:\n    85→                on_step_start(s)\n    86→\n    87→            group_results = _run_parallel_steps(entry, config, run_step, cancel_check)\n    88→            all_results.extend(group_results)\n    89→\n    90→            for r in group_results:\n    91→                on_step_complete(r.step, r)\n    92→\n    93→            on_state_update(_build_state(all_results))\n    94→\n    95→            # If any step in the group failed, halt\n    96→            if any(r.status != StepStatus.PASS for r in group_results):\n    97→                break\n    98→        else:\n    99→            # Sequential step\n   100→            result = _execute_single_step(entry, config, run_step, cancel_check, on_step_start, on_step_complete)\n   101→            all_results.append(result)\n   102→            on_state_update(_build_state(all_results))\n   103→\n   104→            if result.status != StepStatus.PASS:\n   105→                break\n   106→\n   107→    return all_results\n   108→\n   109→\n   110→def _execute_single_step(\n   111→    step: Step,\n   112→    config: PipelineConfig,\n   113→    run_step: StepRunner,\n   114→    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n   115→    on_step_start: Callable[[Step], None] = lambda s: None,\n   116→    on_step_complete: Callable[[Step, StepResult], None] = lambda s, r: None,\n   117→) -> StepResult:\n   118→    \"\"\"Execute a single step with retry logic and gate checking.\"\"\"\n   119→    on_step_start(step)\n   120→    max_attempts = step.retry_limit + 1  # retry_limit=1 means 2 attempts total\n   121→\n   122→    for attempt in range(1, max_attempts + 1):\n   123→        if cancel_check():\n   124→            now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   125→            result = StepResult(\n   126→                step=step,\n   127→                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n   128→                attempt=attempt,\n   129→                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n   130→                started_at=now,\n   131→                finished_at=now,\n   132→            )\n   133→            on_step_complete(step, result)\n   134→            return result\n   135→\n   136→        result = run_step(step, config, cancel_check)\n   137→        result = StepResult(\n   138→            step=result.step,\n   139→            status=result.status,\n   140→            attempt=attempt,\n   141→            gate_failure_reason=result.gate_failure_reason,\n   142→            started_at=result.started_at,\n   143→            finished_at=result.finished_at,\n   144→        )\n   145→\n   146→        # If step has no gate, trust the StepRunner's status\n   147→        if step.gate is None:\n   148→            on_step_complete(step, result)\n   149→            return result\n   150→\n   151→        # If runner already reported failure/timeout, skip gate check\n   152→        if result.status in (StepStatus.TIMEOUT, StepStatus.CANCELLED):\n   153→            on_step_complete(step, result)\n   154→            return result\n   155→\n   156→        # Run gate check\n   157→        passed, reason = gate_passed(step.output_file, step.gate)\n   158→        if passed:\n   159→            result = StepResult(\n   160→                step=step,\n   161→                status=StepStatus.PASS,\n   162→                attempt=attempt,\n   163→                gate_failure_reason=None,\n   164→                started_at=result.started_at,\n   165→                finished_at=result.finished_at,\n   166→            )\n   167→            on_step_complete(step, result)\n   168→            return result\n   169→\n   170→        # Gate failed\n   171→        _log.info(\"Gate failed for step '%s' (attempt %d/%d): %s\", step.id, attempt, max_attempts, reason)\n   172→\n   173→        if attempt < max_attempts:\n   174→            continue  # retry\n   175→\n   176→        # Exhausted retries\n   177→        result = StepResult(\n   178→            step=step,\n   179→            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n   180→            attempt=attempt,\n   181→            gate_failure_reason=reason,\n   182→            started_at=result.started_at,\n   183→            finished_at=result.finished_at,\n   184→        )\n   185→        on_step_complete(step, result)\n   186→        return result\n   187→\n   188→    # Generic step sequencer with retry, gate checks, state updates, and parallel step groups.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/gates.py`\n  - Pure-Python output gate validation against `GateCriteria`.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/process.py`\n  - Manages `claude -p` subprocess lifecycle, timeouts, signals, stdout/stderr files.\n\n### M1 / decomposition\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/deliverables.py`\n  - Detects “behavioral” deliverables and decomposes them into `.a` implement and `.b` verify pairs.\n\n### M2 / invariant registry\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/invariants.py`\n  - Builds mutation/write inventory for detected variables across all deliverables.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/verification_emitter.py`\n  - Emits `invariant_check` deliverables from mutation inventory.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/invariant_pass.py`\n  - Runs the invariant registry sub-pipeline and renders the registry section.\n\n### M2 / FMEA\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/fmea_domains.py`\n  - Enumerates degenerate input domains for behavioral/computational deliverables.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/fmea_classifier.py`\n  - Classifies failure modes using two signals, especially silent corruption detection.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/fmea_promotion.py`\n  - Promotes above-threshold failure modes to `fmea_test` deliverables and enforces Release Gate Rule 1.\n\n### M2 / combined pass\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/combined_m2_pass.py`\n  - Combined M2 pass: invariant registry + FMEA + cross-linking + combined markdown section.\n\n### M3 / guard analysis\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/guard_analyzer.py`\n  - What exists in `models.py` — the data models\n\nFile:\n`/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/models.py`\n\nThis is the shared schema layer. It explicitly avoids importing sprint/roadmap modules.\n\n### `StepStatus`\nEnum with:\n- `PENDING`\n- `PASS`\n- `FAIL`\n- `TIMEOUT`\n- `CANCELLED`\n- `SKIPPED`\n\nHelpers:\n- `is_terminal`\n- `is_success`\n- `is_failure`\n\nThis is the execution-state model for step orchestration, not deliverable analysis.\n\n### `SemanticCheck`\nDataclass:\n- `name: str`\n- `check_fn: Callable[[str], bool]`\n- `failure_message: str`\n\nUsed by strict gate validation.\n\n### `GateCriteria`\nDataclass:\n- `required_frontmatter_fields: list[str]`\n- `min_lines: int`\n- `enforcement_tier: Literal[\"STRICT\", \"STANDARD\", \"LIGHT\", \"EXEMPT\"] = \"STANDARD\"`\n- `semantic_checks: list[SemanticCheck] | None = None`\n\nThis controls the step output gate behavior.\n\n### `Step`\nDataclass:\n- `id: str`\n- `prompt: str`\n- `output_file: Path`\n- `gate: Optional[GateCriteria]`\n- `timeout_seconds: int`\n- `inputs: list[Path] = []`\n- `retry_limit: int = 1`\n- `model: str = \"\"`\n\nThis is the core unit of execution in the generic pipeline executor.\n\n### `StepResult`\nDataclass:\n- `step: Optional[Step]`\n- `status: StepStatus`\n- `attempt: int`\n- `gate_failure_reason: str | None`\n- `started_at`\n- `finished_at`\n\nHelper:\n- `duration_seconds`\n\n### `DeliverableKind`\nEnum:\n- `IMPLEMENT`\n- `VERIFY`\n- `INVARIANT_CHECK`\n- `FMEA_TEST`\n- `GUARD_TEST`\n- `CONTRACT_TEST`\n\nImportant implication: the shared deliverable schema has already been extended to support M2, M3, and M4 generated artifacts.\n\n### `Deliverable`\nDataclass:\n- `id: str`\n- `description: str`\n- `kind: DeliverableKind = DeliverableKind.IMPLEMENT`\n- `metadata: dict = {}`\n\nMethods:\n- `to_dict()`\n- `from_dict()`\n\nThis is the main schema that all analytical passes operate on. The `metadata` field is the extension point used by M2–M4.\n\n### `PipelineConfig`\nDataclass:\n- `work_dir: Path`\n- `dry_run: bool = False`\n- `max_turns: int = 50`\n- `model: str = \"\"`\n- `permission_flag: str = \"--dangerously-skip-permissions\"`\n- `debug: bool = False`\n\nThis is execution config, not analysis config.\n\n### Architectural takeaway from `models.py`\nThe data model already anticipates post-generation analytical passes. Phase 4 does not need to invent new deliverable concepts; it plugs into:\n- `Deliverable`\n- `DeliverableKind.CONTRACT_TEST`\n- `metadata`\n- and the existing pass-style outputs.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Invariant registry output from T02.09\n\nPrimary files:\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/invariant_pass.py`\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/invariants.py`\n\nAnd T02.09 combined integration:\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/combined_m2_pass.py`\n\n### `InvariantRegistryOutput`\nDefined in `invariant_pass.py` with:\n- `entries: list[InvariantEntry]`\n- `generated_deliverables: list[Deliverable]`\n- `warnings: list[str]`\n- `section_markdown: str`\n\n### Invariant pass pipeline\n`run_invariant_registry_pass(deliverables, max_checks_per_variable=5)`:\n\n1. Filters out existing `INVARIANT_CHECK` deliverables for idempotency\n2. Filters to `IMPLEMENT` deliverables\n3. Detects state variables via `detect_state_variables`\n4. Renders markdown section\n\n### Output section format\nThe rendered section includes:\n- header `## Invariant Registry`\n- variable count\n- verification deliverable count\n- table with:\n  - Variable\n  - Scope\n  - Predicate\n  - Mutation Sites\n  - Verification IDs\n\n### `InvariantEntry`\nFrom `invariants.py`:\n- `variable_name`\n- `scope`\n- `invariant_predicate`\n- `mutation_sites`\n- `verification_deliverable_ids`\n\nThe predicate is validated with a constrained grammar, not free-form English.\n\n### T02.09 combined output\n`CombinedM2Output` in `combined_m2_pass.py` includes:\n- `invariant_output: InvariantRegistryOutput`\n- `failure_modes`\n- `promotion_output`\n- `all_generated_deliverables`\n- `section_markdown`\n\nThis means Phase 4 can consume invariant data either:\n- directly from `InvariantRegistryOutput`\n- or from `CombinedM2Output.invariant_output`\n\n### Evidence from prior artifacts\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/.dev/releases/complete/v.2.11-roadmap-v4/tasklist/results/phase-2-result.md`\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/.dev/releases/complete/v.2.11-roadmap-v4/tasklist/checkpoints/CP-P02-END.md`\n\nThese show T02.09 completed and passed.\n\n---\n\n## 5. Shared dataclasses and enums for pipeline execution and deliverables.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/__init__.py`\n  - Public API surface for the pipeline package.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/executor.py`\n  - Generic step sequencer with retry, gate checks, state updates, and parallel step groups.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/gates.py`\n  - Pure-Python output gate validation against `GateCriteria`.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/process.py`\n  - Manages `claude -p` subprocess lifecycle, timeouts, signals, stdout/stderr files.\n\n### M1 / decomposition\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/deliverables.py`\n  - Detects “behavioral” deliverables and decomposes them into `.a` implement and `.b` verify pairs.\n\n### M2 / invariant registry\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/invariants.py`\n  - Defines `MutationSite`, `InvariantEntry`, constrained predicate grammar, duplicate checks.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/state_detector.py`\n  - Detects state variable introductions from deliverable descriptions.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/mutation_inventory.py`\n  - Builds mutation/write inventory for detected variables across all deliverables.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/verification_emitter.py`\n  - Emits `invariant_check` deliverables from mutation inventory.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/invariant_pass.py`\n  - Runs the invariant registry sub-pipeline and renders the registry section.\n\n### M2 / FMEA\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/fmea_domains.py`\n  - Enumerates degenerate input domains for behavioral/computational deliverables.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/fmea_classifier.py`\n  - Classifies failure modes using two signals, especially silent corruption detection.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/fmea_promotion.py`\n  - Promotes above-threshold failure modes to `fmea_test` deliverables and enforces Release Gate Rule 1.\n\n### M2 / combined pass\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/combined_m2_pass.py`\n  - Combined M2 pass: invariant registry + FMEA + cross-linking + combined markdown section.\n\n### M3 / guard analysis\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/guard_analyzer.py`\n  - Detects guard patterns, sentinel values, and type transitions; enumerates states and ambiguity.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/guard_resolution.py`\n  - Emits `guard_test` deliverables and Release Gate Rule 2 warnings for unresolved ambiguity.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/guard_pass.py`\n  - M3 orchestration pass combining guard detection, invariant cross-ref, FMEA elevation, resolution, section rendering.\n\n### M4 / dataflow tracing\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/dataflow_graph.py`\n  - Builds a directed graph of `(deliverable_id, variable_name, operation)` with cycle/dead-write detection.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/contract_extractor.py`\n  - Extracts implicit writer/reader contracts from cross-milestone dataflow edges.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/conflict_detector.py`\n  - Detects semantic divergence between writer and reader, including scope/type/completeness mismatch.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/dataflow_pass.py`\n  - M4 orchestration pass that builds graph, extracts contracts, detects conflicts, emits `contract_test` deliverables, and conditionally skips below threshold.\n\n### Other\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/executor.py`\n  - Base runner infrastructure used by consumers.\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/__pycache__/`\n  - Bytecode cache, not architecturally relevant.\n\n---\n\n## 2. What exists in `models.py` — the data models\n\nFile:\n`/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/models.py`\n\nThis is the shared schema layer. It explicitly avoids importing sprint/roadmap modules.\n\n### `StepStatus`\nEnum with:\n- `PENDING`\n- `PASS`\n- `FAIL`\n- `TIMEOUT`\n- `CANCELLED`\n- `SKIPPED`\n\nHelpers:\n- `is_terminal`\n- `is_success`\n- `is_failure`\n\nThis is the execution-state model for step orchestration, not deliverable analysis.\n\n### `SemanticCheck`\nDataclass:\n- `name: str`\n- `check_fn: Callable[[str], bool]`\n- `failure_message: str`\n\nUsed by strict gate validation.\n\n### `GateCriteria`\nDataclass:\n- `required_frontmatter_fields: list[str]`\n- `min_lines: int`\n- `enforcement_tier: Literal[\"STRICT\", \"STANDARD\", \"LIGHT\", \"EXEMPT\"] = \"STANDARD\"`\n- `semantic_checks: list[SemanticCheck] | None = None`\n\nThis controls the step output gate behavior.\n\n### `Step`\nDataclass:\n- `id: str`\n- `prompt: str`\n- `output_file: Path`\n- `gate: Optional[GateCriteria]`\n- `timeout_seconds: int`\n- `inputs: list[Path] = []`\n- `retry_limit: int = 1`\n- `model: str = \"\"`\n\nThis is the core unit of execution in the generic pipeline executor.\n\n### `StepResult`\nDataclass:\n- `step: Optional[Step]`\n- `status: StepStatus`\n- `attempt: int`\n- `gate_failure_reason: str | None`\n- `started_at`\n- `finished_at`\n\nHelper:\n- `duration_seconds`\n\n### `DeliverableKind`\nEnum:\n- `IMPLEMENT`\n- `VERIFY`\n- `INVARIANT_CHECK`\n- `FMEA_TEST`\n- `GUARD_TEST`\n- `CONTRACT_TEST`\n\nImportant implication: the shared deliverable schema has already been extended to support M2, M3, and M4 generated artifacts.\n\n### `Deliverable`\nDataclass:\n- `id: str`\n- `description: str`\n- `kind: DeliverableKind = DeliverableKind.IMPLEMENT`\n- `metadata: dict = {}`\n\nMethods:\n- `to_dict()`\n- `from_dict()`\n\nThis is the main schema that all analytical passes operate on. The `metadata` field is the extension point used by M2–M4.\n\n### `PipelineConfig`\nDataclass:\n- `work_dir: Path`\n- `dry_run: bool = False`\n- `max_turns: int = 50`\n- `model: str = \"\"`\n- `permission_flag: str = \"--dangerously-skip-permissions\"`\n- `debug: bool = False`\n\nThis is execution config, not analysis config.\n\n### Architectural takeaway from `models.py`\nThe data model already anticipates post-generation analytical passes. Phase 4 does not need to invent new deliverable concepts; it plugs into:\n- `Deliverable`\n- `DeliverableKind.CONTRACT_TEST`\n- `metadata`\n- and the existing pass-style outputs.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Invariant registry output from T02.09\n\nPrimary files:\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/invariant_pass.py`\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/invariants.py`\n\nAnd T02.09 combined integration:\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/combined_m2_pass.py`\n\n### `InvariantRegistryOutput`\nDefined in `invariant_pass.py` with:\n- `entries: list[InvariantEntry]`\n- `generated_deliverables: list[Deliverable]`\n- `warnings: list[str]`\n- `section_markdown: str`\n\n### Invariant pass pipeline\n`run_invariant_registry_pass(deliverables, max_checks_per_variable=5)`:\n\n1. Filters out existing `INVARIANT_CHECK` deliverables for idempotency\n2. Filters to `IMPLEMENT` deliverables\n3. Detects state variables via `detect_state_variables`\n4. Generates mutation inventory across all deliverables\n5. Builds `InvariantEntry` objects\n6. Emits verification deliverables via `emit_invariant_check_deliverables`\n7. Checks duplicate variables\n8. Renders markdown section\n\n### Output section format\nThe rendered section includes:\n- header `## Invariant Registry`\n- variable count\n- verification deliverable count\n- table with:\n  - Variable\n  - Scope\n  - Predicate\n  - Mutation Sites\n  - Verification IDs\n\n### `InvariantEntry`\nFrom `invariants.py`:\n- `variable_name`\n- `scope`\n- `invariant_predicate`\n- `mutation_sites`\n- `verification_deliverable_ids`\n\nThe predicate is validated with a constrained grammar, not free-form English.\n\n### T02.09 combined output\n`CombinedM2Output` in `combined_m2_pass.py` includes:\n- `invariant_output: InvariantRegistryOutput`\n- `failure_modes`\n- `promotion_output`\n- `all_generated_deliverables`\n- `section_markdown`\n\nThis means Phase 4 can consume invariant data either:\n- directly from `InvariantRegistryOutput`\n- or from `CombinedM2Output.invariant_output`\n\n### Evidence from prior artifacts\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/.dev/releases/complete/v.2.11-roadmap-v4/tasklist/results/phase-2-result.md`\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/.dev/releases/complete/v.2.11-roadmap-v4/tasklist/checkpoints/CP-P02-END.md`\n\nThese show T02.09 completed and passed.\n\n---\n\n## 5. Guard analysis output from T03.03\n\nPrimary files:\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/guard_pass.py`\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/guard_analyzer.py`\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/guard_resolution.py`\n\n### `GuardAnalysisOutput`\nDefined in `guard_pass.py`:\n- `detections: list[GuardDetection]`\n- `resolution: GuardResolutionOutput`\n- `invariant_cross_refs: dict[str, InvariantEntry | None]`\n- `fmea_elevations: list[str]`\n- `section_markdown: str`\n\nProperty:\n- `can_advance_to_m4`\n\nThis is the direct Phase-3-to-Phase-4 handoff structure.\n\n### What `run_guard_analysis_pass()` does\nInputs:\n- `deliverables`\n- `invariant_output`\n- `fmea_severity_map`\n\nPipeline:\n1. Detect guards\n2. Cross-reference guard variables against invariant registry\n3. Check FMEA severity and elevate ambiguous guards to silent corruption if severity is high/critical\n4. Resolve guards into deliverables + warnings\n5. Render markdown section\n\n### `GuardResolutionOutput`\nFrom `guard_resolution.py`:\n- `guard_test_deliverables`\n- `gate_warnings`\n- `section_markdown`\n\nProperties:\n- `has_blocking_warnings`\n- `can_advance`\n\n### Release Gate Rule 2\nGuard ambiguity is blocking until owner/risk resolution exists. It:\n1. Counts milestones from all deliverables\n2. Applies conditional threshold check (default: 6+ milestones)\n3. Builds data flow graph (T04.01)\n4. Extracts implicit contracts (T04.02)\n5. Detects conflicts (T04.03)\n6. Emits `contract_test` deliverables\n7. Renders markdown section\n\n## Conditional Threshold\n\n- **6+ milestones** (default): Full data flow tracing with contracts, conflicts, and `contract_test` deliverables\n- **Below threshold**: Skip summary referencing M2 Invariant Registry, zero `contract_test` deliverables\n- **`--force-dataflow`**: Overrides threshold, enables full tracing regardless\n- **`--dataflow-threshold N`**: Configures the threshold (default: 6)\n\n## Output Section Format\n\nThe `section_markdown` includes:\n- Milestone count, node count, edge count, cross-milestone edge count\n- Cycle warnings (if any)\n- Dead write warnings with deliverable IDs\n- Implicit contracts table (Variable, Writer, Reader, Semantics, Assumption, Confidence)\n- Conflicts table (Variable, Kind, Severity, Description)\n- Generated `contract_test` deliverables list\n\n## Public API\n\nExported from `superclaude.cli.pipeline`:\n- `DataFlowTracingOutput` - Output dataclass\n- `run_dataflow_tracing_pass()` - M4 orchestration function\n- `DataFlowGraph`, `DataFlowNode`, `DataFlowEdge`, `NodeOperation` - Graph types\n- `ImplicitContract`, `extract_implicit_contracts` - Contract extraction\n- `ConflictKind`, `ConflictDetection`, `detect_conflicts` - Conflict detection\n- `build_dataflow_graph` - Graph construction\n\n## Implementation Files\n\n- `src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/dataflow_pass.py` -
